Lets hope you don't need to defend yourself because all of the weapons lockers are empty in the Weapons Bay. Only a few clips of ammo and loose cartridges are scattered on the floor.\n\nOne of the locker doors creaks, then suddenly swings open, and a crewmate falls out of the locker to the floor... dead.\n\nYou search your crewmate and the rest of the lockers without finding any fuel rods.\n\nThe Weapons Bay only has one exit back to the [[Passageway]].\n\nYou have collected <<print $count>> of 3 fuel rods.
Congratulations!!! You've now restored life support and have enough fuel to return to Earth. The power also activates the emergency defence system, which teleports the two aliens to their point of origin. You awaken from being knocked unconscious on the bridge of the starship DHUM-150. The last Captain's log, that's looping over and over on a monitor in the background, reports that fugitive aliens, from the planet Ghoti, boarded your ship for some unknown reason. A quick status report by the on-board computer reveals they stole the fission reactor fuel. Without three rods of fuel, minimum, your ship is dead in space.\n\nExplore the ship to see if the aliens dropped any rods in their getaway. Once you've found three rods, take them to the Engine Room to restart the engines.\n\nWarning... the computer informs you that two aliens are still aboard somewhere!!!\n\nYou can take the lift to the next floor [[down|Galley]].\n<<nobr>>\n<<if $count < 1>>\n<<set $count = 0>>\n<<set $ssq = false>>\n<<set $mb = false>>\n<<set $psb = false>>\n<<set $joke_seen = false>>\n<<endif>>\n<<endnobr>>\nYou have collected <<print $count>> of 3 fuel rods.
<<if $count is 3>>\nGreat, now insert the fuel cannister containing the three rods into the reactor chamber and push the big [[red button|Red Button]].\n<<else>>\nKeep searching! You've only found <<print $count>> of 3 rods so far.\n\nDid I mention that the reactor also powers life support? Hurry to find the remaining fuel rods so you don't suffocate. No use trying to use the escape pod either. It was jettisoned by accident during the last Space Militia raid.\n\nReturn via the lift to the [[Passageway]] above.\n<<endif>>
